# codex-memory Status

更新时间：2026-05-26

## 当前结论

- `CM-1181 STARTUP_EXPLICIT_REBUILD_RECOVERY_POLICY_PLAN` 已完成 docs-only 计划，状态为 `CM1181_STARTUP_EXPLICIT_REBUILD_RECOVERY_POLICY_PLAN_COMPLETED_NOT_IMPLEMENTED_NOT_READY`：当前已有 `MemoryWriteService.rebuildMissingDiaryProjections(...)` 与 `MemoryWriteReconcileWorker` 的 `dryRun/runOnce/start/status` building blocks，但没有统一 startup policy 规定哪些 recovery 可自动检查、哪些只能 dry-run、哪些必须 explicit approval。CM-1181 计划的边界是 startup 可 inspect/report selected sanitized posture，不能 silent diary rebuild，不能 silent reconcile apply，不能改 config/watchdog/startup persistence；apply/rebuild/reconcile 仍需后续 exact source/test slice 和真实 store 场景的 separate explicit approval。本次未实现 startup recovery，未启动/安装 worker，未执行 rebuild/reconcile apply，未写 durable memory/audit，未声明 readiness 或 reliability。
- `CM-1180 SQLITE_SCHEMA_VERSION_STARTUP_GATE_PLAN` 已完成 docs-only 计划，状态为 `CM1180_SQLITE_SCHEMA_VERSION_STARTUP_GATE_PLAN_COMPLETED_NOT_IMPLEMENTED_NOT_READY`：当前 `SqliteShadowStore.ensureReady()` 会 `CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS` 并通过 `ensureColumn(... ALTER TABLE ...)` opportunistic repair 已知列，但没有 `PRAGMA user_version` / schema version registry / unknown-future-version fail-closed startup gate。CM-1180 只把 future gate 固化为计划：定义 expected schema version、只读 inspection、known additive repair evidence、unknown future version hard stop、sanitized health/overview facts。未实现 gate，未执行 SQLite migration/`ALTER TABLE`，未改 startup/config/watchdog，未触碰真实 memory stores，未声明 readiness 或 reliability。
- `CM-1179 NO_TOKEN_SEARCH_EVIDENCE_REVIEW` 已完成对 CM-1177/CM-1178 的 actual evidence review，状态为 `CM1179_NO_TOKEN_SEARCH_EVIDENCE_REVIEW_BLOCKER_DOWNGRADED_NOT_RELIABLE_NOT_READY`：接受的窄证据是 no-token HTTP `search_memory` 已被验证不会触发 sync、candidate cache get/set、recall/read-policy audit、embedding-cache flush、external embedding/rerank provider，且 `include_content=true` raw-content 请求会在 HTTP boundary 返回 `403`、早于 tool execution。允许的降级仅限 covered public HTTP no-token `search_memory` side-effect/raw-content blocker；不声明 full no-token governance closure、`memory recall reliable`、`memory write reliable`、runtime/RC/production readiness。剩余缺口：no-token `memory_overview` selected-output posture、SQLite schema migration/version startup gate、startup explicit rebuild/recovery policy、完整 lifecycle transition log。
- `CM-1178 NO_TOKEN_RAW_CONTENT_READ_CLOSURE` 已完成第一段 no-token raw-content read closure，状态为 `CM1178_NO_TOKEN_RAW_CONTENT_READ_CLOSURE_VALIDATED_NOT_READY`：HTTP JSON-RPC no-token 边界现在拒绝 `search_memory` 且 `arguments.include_content === true` 的请求，返回 HTTP `403`，避免 no-token caller 通过 public HTTP MCP surface 请求 raw memory content；authorized bearer-token `search_memory` 行为不变。验证通过：`node --check src\adapters\codex-mcp\http.js`；`node --check tests\mcp-http.test.js`；`node --test tests\mcp-http.test.js` `18/18`；`node --test tests\mcp-http.test.js tests\mcp-contract.test.js tests\phase-a-services.test.js` `35/35`；ledger consistency；docs validation；`git diff --check`；full `npm test` `2787/2787`（第一次 full run 在 `124s` 超时且没有 pass/fail summary，重跑通过）。本次未改变 public MCP schema，未触碰真实 memory stores/raw `.jsonl`，未调用 provider/API，未修改 `.env`/config/watchdog/startup/dependencies，未执行 migration/import/export/backup/restore，未 push，不声明 production readiness、write reliability 或 recall reliability。剩余缺口：no-token `memory_overview` selected-output hardening 是否需要继续确认、SQLite schema migration/version startup gate、startup explicit rebuild/recovery policy、完整 lifecycle transition log 仍未处理。
- `CM-1177 READONLY_SYNCING_SEARCH_SEMANTIC_SPLIT` 已完成第一段 readonly/syncing search boundary runtime-kernel 切片，状态为 `CM1177_READONLY_SYNCING_SEARCH_SEMANTIC_SPLIT_VALIDATED_NOT_READY`：`CandidateGenerator.generate(...)` 在 `readOnly=true` 时现在连 candidate cache read 都会绕过，避免 no-token/readonly search 更新 candidate-cache 命中元数据；既有 `KnowledgeBaseRecallPipeline` readonly 语义继续阻止 `KnowledgeBaseSyncService.syncTarget(...)`，既有 app-level guard 继续阻止 readonly search 写 recall audit / read-policy audit，既有 vector/rerank readonly 语义继续避免 external embedding/rerank provider 与 embedding-cache flush。HTTP no-token regression 已加强为若触发 sync、candidate cache get/set、recall/read-policy audit、embedding flush、external embedding/rerank provider 即失败；phase-B sync/cache/rerank regression 仍证明默认 authorized syncing search 可以正常 sync/cache/audit。验证通过：`node --check src\recall\CandidateGenerator.js`；`node --check tests\mcp-http.test.js`；`node --test tests\mcp-http.test.js tests\phase-b-sync-cache-rerank.test.js` `33/33`；full `npm test` `2786/2786`。本次未改变 public MCP schema，未触碰真实 memory stores/raw `.jsonl`，未调用 provider/API，未修改 `.env`/config/watchdog/startup/dependencies，未执行 migration/import/export/backup/restore，未 push，不声明 production readiness、write reliability 或 recall reliability。剩余缺口：broader no-token read closure、SQLite schema migration/version startup gate、startup explicit rebuild/recovery policy、完整 lifecycle transition log 仍未处理。
- `CM-1176 DIARY_PROJECTION_REBUILD_FROM_SQLITE_AUTHORITY` 已完成第一段 diary projection reconcile/rebuild runtime-kernel 切片，状态为 `CM1176_DIARY_PROJECTION_REBUILD_FROM_SQLITE_AUTHORITY_VALIDATED_NOT_READY`：新增内部 `MemoryWriteService.rebuildMissingDiaryProjections(...)`，它扫描已 SQLite committed 且带 `record_json` 的 write manifests，跳过已有 `filePath/relativePath` 的记录，对缺失 diary projection 的记录从 SQLite authoritative record 重写 diary 文件，然后刷新 SQLite manifest record、shadow record、vector index 与 chunks，并通过既有 write audit/manifest audited path 记录 selected lifecycle。`SqliteShadowStore.updateMemoryWriteManifestRecord(...)` 在 `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` 内同步更新 manifest `record_json` 与 shadow record；新增 manifest 列表方法只服务内部 rebuild，不扩 public MCP。新增 temp-local runtime test 先合成 diary 写失败导致 `accepted/degraded + filePath=null`，确认 diary 中没有记录，再恢复 diary writer 调用 rebuild，验证 manifest 从 degraded 回到 committed、manifest record 获得 `filePath/relativePath`、shadow record/diary/search/overview 一致。验证通过：source/test syntax checks；`node --test tests\durable-write-kernel-idempotency-runtime.test.js` `7/7`；相邻 restart/reconcile/reliability/worker bundle `37/37`；full `npm test` `2786/2786`。本次未改变 public MCP schema，未触碰真实 memory stores，未调用 provider/API，未修改 `.env`/config/watchdog/startup/dependencies，未执行 real rebuild/migration/import/export/backup/restore，未 push，不声明 production readiness、write reliability 或 recall reliability。剩余缺口：rebuild 仍是显式内部方法，不是 startup 自动恢复；lifecycle 仍不是完整 transition log；readonly/syncing search split、no-token read closure、SQLite schema migration/version gate 仍未处理。
- `CM-1175 WRITE_MANIFEST_LIFECYCLE_STATE_SPLIT` 已完成第一段 manifest lifecycle 显式化，状态为 `CM1175_WRITE_MANIFEST_LIFECYCLE_STATE_SPLIT_VALIDATED_NOT_READY`：在 CM-1174 SQLite authoritative write 竖切片基础上，新增 `memory_write_manifests.projected_at` 与 `audited_at`，并让 `attachRecordToMemoryWriteManifest(...)` 在 SQLite authoritative record 落地时设置 `committed_at`，但保持 `status='pending'` 以保留 crash-window recovery gate；`finalizeMemoryWriteManifest(...)` 在 projection 完成后设置 `projected_at`，`MemoryWriteService.writeAuditAndMarkMemoryWriteManifestAudited(...)` 在 write audit 成功后设置 `audited_at` 并更新 manifest `result_json`。`memory_overview` 的 shadow health 现在暴露 selected `writeManifest.lifecycle.sqliteCommitted/projected/audited/pendingRecovery` counters；selected write-manifest audit 增加 sanitized lifecycle booleans。Temp-local runtime tests 现在验证正常 write 的 `committed/projected/audited` 完整链、diary projection failure 的 degraded audited chain、pending manifest with SQLite authority 的 `pendingRecovery` 可见、cancel policy 会保留带 manifest `record_json` 的 recoverable pending manifest、recovery 后转为 projected/audited、duplicate canonical replay 保持同一 memory id。Changed-scope re-review 发现并修复旧 cancel policy 只看 diary、可能误 cancel `pending + record_json` 的问题。验证通过：source/test syntax checks；`node --test tests\durable-write-kernel-idempotency-runtime.test.js` `6/6`；audit/restart/reconcile/reliability/worker adjacent bundle `42/42`；full `npm test` final rerun `2785/2785`（窄修后一次 full run 曾出现非复现 `2` fail，随后 failure extraction rerun 与 summary rerun 均通过）。本次未改变 public MCP schema，未触碰真实 memory stores，未调用 provider/API，未修改 `.env`/config/watchdog/startup/dependencies，未 push，不声明 production readiness、write reliability 或 recall reliability。剩余缺口：状态机仍是兼容式 timestamp/lifecycle counters，不是完整独立 transition log；diary projection reconcile/rebuild、readonly/syncing search split、no-token read closure、SQLite schema migration/version gate 仍未处理。
- `CM-1174 SQLITE_AUTHORITATIVE_RECORD_BEFORE_DIARY_PROJECTION` 已完成第一段 runtime-kernel 竖切片，状态为 `CM1174_SQLITE_AUTHORITATIVE_RECORD_BEFORE_DIARY_PROJECTION_VALIDATED_NOT_READY`：当前源码已确认 CM-1155..CM-1165 `record_json`，`SqliteShadowStore.attachRecordToMemoryWriteManifest(...)` 在 `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` 事务内把 authoritative record upsert 到 SQLite 并绑定 pending manifest；`MemoryWriteService.record()` 现在在 diary projection 前先写 SQLite authoritative record，diary 失败时不再丢失权威记录，而是返回 accepted/degraded、`filePath=null`，继续允许 SQLite/chunk/vector projection；`recoverPendingWriteManifests(...)` 会优先使用 manifest `record_json`，没有 diary record 时也能从 SQLite authoritative record 恢复 projections；`KnowledgeBaseSyncService` 在 diary sync/prune 时保留带 active write manifest 且无 `filePath` 的 SQLite-authoritative 记录，同时不阻止普通 diary 删除后的 stale prune。新增 temp-local runtime integration tests 验证 `record_memory -> search_memory -> overview/health` 仍一致、diary projection failure 后 SQLite record/chunks 可被 default syncing search 与 read-only search 查到、pending manifest 可在无 diary 情况下从 SQLite record 恢复、duplicate canonical write replay 同一 memory id。验证通过：source/test syntax checks；`node --test tests\durable-write-kernel-idempotency-runtime.test.js` `6/6`；`phase-b-sync-cache-rerank` + durable targeted bundle `22/22`；相邻 `memory-write-restart-durability-temp-local-evidence` `7/7`；相邻 `memory-write-reconcile-service` + `memory-write-reliability-temp-local-evidence` `11/11`；`memory-write-reconcile-worker` `19/19`；full `npm test` final rerun `2785/2785`（中间一次 full run 曾出现非复现失败，后续 failure extraction rerun 与 summary rerun 均通过）；`git diff --check` 通过。本次未扩 public MCP schema，未修改 `.env`/config/watchdog/startup/dependencies，未触碰真实 memory stores，未调用 provider/API，未 push，且不声明 production readiness、write reliability 或 recall reliability。剩余缺口：manifest 状态机尚未完全拆成 `pending -> committed -> projected -> audited`，diary projection reconcile/rebuild 仍未实现，search readonly/syncing 语义尚未显式拆分，no-token read 和 schema migration/version gate 尚未处理。

- `CM-1058 MEMORY_WRITE_MEMORY_ID_RECONCILE_CLEANUP_TEMP_LOCAL_EVIDENCE` 已完成并保持 temp-local memory-id reconcile cleanup isolation / not reliable / not ready：更新 `tests/memory-write-degraded-cleanup-temp-local-evidence.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1058_MEMORY_WRITE_MEMORY_ID_RECONCILE_CLEANUP_TEMP_LOCAL_EVIDENCE.md`。该 slice 不改 runtime source，只在 isolated temp-local degraded cleanup harness 中写入两条 synthetic degraded accepted process records，确认每条写入各留下 `chunks` 与 `vector` 两个 residual tasks，总计 `reconcileCount=4`。随后只对第一条 synthetic memory id 执行 projection/cache cleanup，确认 SQLite record count 保持 `1`、`reconcileCount` 仍为 `4`；显式调用 `clearReconcileTasks(firstMemoryId)` 后，`reconcileCount` 降为 `2` 且剩余 queued tasks 全部仍绑定第二条 memory id；重复清理第一条 memory id 不会误删第二条 residuals；最终调用 `clearReconcileTasks(secondMemoryId)` 才清零 residual queue。两条 diary files 与 write-audit file 仍保留可见。验证通过：test syntax check、targeted degraded cleanup test file `4/4`、adjacent write cleanup/reconcile/MCP regression bundle `44/44`、full `npm test` `2508/2508`。该 slice 不执行 true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不新增 cleanup tool，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、real cleanup safe、real rollback safe、rollback readiness、runtime readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-1057 MEMORY_WRITE_STORE_KIND_RECONCILE_CLEANUP_TEMP_LOCAL_EVIDENCE` 已完成并保持 temp-local store-kind reconcile cleanup posture / not reliable / not ready：更新 `tests/memory-write-degraded-cleanup-temp-local-evidence.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1057_MEMORY_WRITE_STORE_KIND_RECONCILE_CLEANUP_TEMP_LOCAL_EVIDENCE.md`。该 slice 不改 runtime source，只在 isolated temp-local degraded cleanup harness 中写入一条 synthetic degraded accepted process record，确认 vector/chunk projection failures 留下 exactly two reconcile residual tasks（`chunks` 与 `vector`）。在 partial projection cleanup 后，显式调用 `clearReconcileTasks(memoryId, 'vector')` 只清掉 `vector` residual，使 `reconcileCount` 从 `2` 降到 `1`，并证明剩余 task 仍是 `chunks`；重复清 `vector` 不会误删 `chunks`；随后调用 `clearReconcileTasks(memoryId, 'chunks')` 才清零 residual queue。验证通过：test syntax check、targeted degraded cleanup test file `3/3`、adjacent write cleanup/reconcile/MCP regression bundle `43/43`、full `npm test` `2507/2507`。该 slice 不执行 true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不新增 cleanup tool，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、real cleanup safe、real rollback safe、rollback readiness、runtime readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。

- `CM-1055 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_STOP_RETURN_OPTIONS_GUARD` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile worker stop return options guard / not reliable / not ready：更新 `src/core/MemoryWriteReconcileWorker.js`、`tests/memory-write-reconcile-worker.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1055_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_STOP_RETURN_OPTIONS_GUARD.md`。该 slice 修正一个 operator-facing 停止返回值审计缺口：`stop()` 现在在 `stopped` 与 `not_running` 两种返回中都包含 active bounded options（`intervalMs`、`limit`、`dryRun`、`maxRuns`）和 `runCount`，但不返回 `lastResultSummary`。测试证明显式 `start({ dryRun: true, limit: 7, maxRuns: 3 })` 完成一轮 manual tick 后，`stop()` 清掉下一轮 timer，并返回 active options（`intervalMs=250`、`limit=7`、`dryRun=true`、`maxRuns=3`、`runCount=1`）；第二次 `stop()` 返回 `not_running` 且保留同一 bounded options/runCount；返回值不暴露 raw synthetic memory id，停止后不再 replay。验证通过：source/test syntax checks、CM-1055 targeted worker test `19/19`、adjacent worker/service/write reliability/MCP regression bundle `41/41`、full `npm test` `2505/2505`。该 slice 不执行 temp/true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不执行 runtime observe，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic startup worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、startup reconcile safe、runtime readiness、rollback readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-1054 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_ALREADY_RUNNING_START_GUARD` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile worker already-running start guard / not reliable / not ready：更新 `src/core/MemoryWriteReconcileWorker.js`、`tests/memory-write-reconcile-worker.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1054_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_ALREADY_RUNNING_START_GUARD.md`。该 slice 修正一个 operator-facing 状态一致性缺口：`start()` 在 worker already running 时现在返回 active `maxRuns`，并用 unit-level manual scheduler 证明第二次 `start({ dryRun: true, limit: 99, maxRuns: 9, intervalMs: 500 })` 不会重配当前 run、不重置 `runCount`、不新增 timer，返回的是原 active options（`intervalMs=250`、`limit=6`、`dryRun=false`、`maxRuns=2`）。第一轮 tick 使用原 options，之后因 `maxRuns=2` 保持 running 并只排一个 next timer，status 不暴露 raw synthetic memory id。验证通过：source/test syntax checks、CM-1054 targeted worker test `18/18`、adjacent worker/service/write reliability/MCP regression bundle `37/37`、full `npm test` `2504/2504`。该 slice 不执行 temp/true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不执行 runtime observe，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic startup worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、startup reconcile safe、runtime readiness、rollback readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-1053 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_STOP_WITHOUT_CLEARTIMEOUT_GUARD` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile worker stop without clearTimeout guard / not reliable / not ready：更新 `tests/memory-write-reconcile-worker.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1053_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_STOP_WITHOUT_CLEARTIMEOUT_GUARD.md`。该 slice 不改 runtime source，只补一个 scheduler degradation unit proof：当 injected scheduler 提供 `setTimeout` 但没有 `clearTimeout` 时，`stop()` 无法取消外部残留 timer，但 worker 已将 `running=false`、`timer=null`；后续 stale callback 进入 `tick()` 后因 stopped 状态立即 no-op，不执行 replay、不重排 timer。测试证明显式 `start({ dryRun: false, limit: 6, maxRuns: 3 })` 排出一个 timer，`stop()` 后状态为 stopped/no timer/no in-flight/runCount `0`，flush stale callback 后 replay calls 仍为 `0`、最终状态仍 stopped/no timer/runCount `0`、`lastResultSummary=null` 且 status 不暴露 raw synthetic memory id。验证通过：test syntax check、CM-1053 targeted worker test `17/17`、adjacent worker/service/write reliability/MCP regression bundle `36/36`、full `npm test` `2503/2503`。该 slice 不执行 temp/true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不执行 runtime observe，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic startup worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、startup reconcile safe、runtime readiness、rollback readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-1052 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_SCHEDULER_UNAVAILABLE_START_GUARD` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile worker scheduler-unavailable start guard / not reliable / not ready：更新 `src/core/MemoryWriteReconcileWorker.js`、`tests/memory-write-reconcile-worker.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1052_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_SCHEDULER_UNAVAILABLE_START_GUARD.md`。该 slice 只修正一个 operator-facing 返回状态缺口：当 injected scheduler 缺少 `setTimeout` 时，`scheduleNext()` 已 fail-closed 并把 worker 置为 stopped，但 `start()` 返回值过去仍可能报告 `started/running=true`；现在 `start()` 在调度失败后返回 `start_failed/running=false` 和 bounded `lastResultSummary`。测试证明 scheduler unavailable 不会触发 replay，`getStatus()` 为 stopped/no timer/no in-flight/runCount `0`，返回摘要与状态摘要一致且不暴露 raw scheduler error。验证通过：source/test syntax checks、CM-1052 targeted worker test `16/16`、adjacent worker/service/write reliability/MCP regression bundle `35/35`、full `npm test` `2502/2502`。该 slice 不执行 temp/true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不执行 runtime observe，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic startup worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、startup reconcile safe、runtime readiness、rollback readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-1051 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_RESTART_STATE_RESET_GUARD` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile worker restart state reset / not reliable / not ready：更新 `src/core/MemoryWriteReconcileWorker.js`、`tests/memory-write-reconcile-worker.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1051_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_RESTART_STATE_RESET_GUARD.md`。该 slice 只做一个很小的 worker 状态卫生修正：`start()` 在显式开启新一轮 worker run 时清空上一轮 `lastResult`，避免 stop 后重新 start、首个新 tick 尚未执行时的状态面板展示旧 replay summary。测试先执行 `start({ dryRun: false, limit: 3, maxRuns: 1 })` 并完成一轮 scheduled tick，确认第一轮有 bounded sanitized `lastResultSummary`；随后再次显式 `start({ dryRun: true, limit: 8, maxRuns: 1 })`，确认 restart pre-tick 状态为 `runCount=0`、`timerScheduled=true`、new options 生效且 `lastResultSummary=null`；第二轮 tick 后确认使用新 options 并生成新的 bounded summary，status 不暴露 raw synthetic memory id。验证通过：source/test syntax checks、CM-1051 targeted worker test `15/15`、adjacent worker/service/write reliability/MCP regression bundle `34/34`、full `npm test` `2501/2501`。该 slice 不执行 temp/true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不执行 runtime observe，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic startup worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、startup reconcile safe、runtime readiness、rollback readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-1050 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_STOP_INFLIGHT_RESCHEDULE_GUARD` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile worker stop-in-flight / not reliable / not ready：更新 `tests/memory-write-reconcile-worker.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1050_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_STOP_INFLIGHT_RESCHEDULE_GUARD.md`。该 slice 不改 runtime source，仅用 unit-level manual scheduler 与 delayed replay Promise 证明 default-disabled internal worker 在 scheduled tick in-flight 时被显式 `stop()` 后不会在 replay settle 后重新排 timer。测试启动 worker `start({ dryRun: false, limit: 5 })`，flush 一轮 scheduled tick 后确认 `tickInFlight=true` 且当前无 timer；随后调用 `stop()`，确认 worker stopped、`timerScheduled=false`、manual scheduler active timers `0`；释放 delayed replay 后，worker 仍 stopped/no timer/no in-flight，`runCount=1`，无第二次 replay call，无可 flush 的新 timer，status 不暴露 raw synthetic memory id。验证通过：test syntax check、CM-1050 targeted worker test `14/14`、adjacent worker/service/write reliability/MCP regression bundle `33/33`、full `npm test` `2500/2500`。该 slice 不执行 temp/true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不执行 runtime observe，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic startup worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、startup reconcile safe、runtime readiness、rollback readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-1049 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_MAXRUNS_RESIDUAL_QUEUE_TEMP_LOCAL_EVIDENCE` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile worker maxRuns residual queue / not reliable / not ready：更新 `tests/memory-write-reconcile-worker.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1049_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_MAXRUNS_RESIDUAL_QUEUE_TEMP_LOCAL_EVIDENCE.md`。该 slice 不改 runtime source，在 isolated temp-local harness 中使用真实本地 `DiaryStore`、`SqliteShadowStore`、`VectorIndexStore`、`AuditLogStore` 与 `ChunkIndexingService`，通过两条 synthetic degraded accepted writes 构造四个 deterministic vector/chunk replay tasks。测试显式启动 default-disabled internal worker：`start({ dryRun: false, limit: 2, maxRuns: 2 })`，并用 manual scheduler 执行两轮 scheduled ticks；每轮 scanned `2`、replayed `1`、cleared `1`、failed `1`，vector replay 成功而 chunk replay 失败。第二轮后 worker 因 `maxRuns=2` 停止，`runCount=2`、`timerScheduled=false`、manual scheduler active timers `0`，reconcile queue count 保持 `2`，即两个 failed chunk tasks 仍然保留；worker status 不暴露 raw memory ids 或 raw projection error text。随后单独显式调用 healthy worker `runOnce({ dryRun: false, limit: 2 })` drain 剩余两个 chunk tasks，reconcile queue count 回到 `0`，chunk count 至少为 `2`。验证通过：test syntax check、CM-1049 targeted worker test `13/13`、adjacent worker/service/write reliability/MCP regression bundle `32/32`、full `npm test` `2499/2499`。该 slice 不执行 true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不执行 runtime observe，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic startup worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、startup reconcile safe、runtime readiness、rollback readiness、governance closure、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。

- `CM-1038 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_BOUNDED_LOOP_DURABILITY` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile worker bounded loop / not reliable / not ready：更新 `tests/memory-write-reconcile-worker.test.js`，新增 `docs/CM1038_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_WORKER_BOUNDED_LOOP_DURABILITY.md`。该 slice 不改 runtime source，只用 manual scheduler 证明 default-disabled internal worker 在显式 `start({ dryRun: true, maxRuns: 2 })` 后会执行 bounded scheduled loop：第一轮 replay 被人为保持 pending 时，`tickInFlight=true`，重入 `tick()` 不会再次调用 `replayPending(...)`；第一轮 replay 释放后，worker 记录 bounded failure summary 且 status JSON 不暴露 raw synthetic memory id；第二轮 scheduled tick 使用相同 bounded options 执行，随后因 `maxRuns=2` 停止。验证通过：test syntax check、CM-1038 targeted worker test `7/7`、adjacent worker/service/write reliability/MCP regression bundle `26/26`、full `npm test` `2490/2490`、ledger consistency、docs validation、diff check 与 no-overclaim/public-MCP scans。该 slice 不执行 true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不执行 runtime observe，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic startup worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、startup reconcile safe、runtime observe safe、real cleanup safe、real rollback safe、governance closure、long-run durability、rollback readiness、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。

- `CM-1035 MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_SERVICE_INTERNAL_IDLE` 已完成并保持 internal write reconcile service / not reliable / not ready：新增 `src/core/MemoryWriteReconcileService.js`、`tests/memory-write-reconcile-service.test.js` 和 `docs/CM1035_MEMORY_WRITE_RECONCILE_SERVICE_INTERNAL_IDLE.md`，并在 `src/app.js` 仅挂载内部 `app.services.memoryWriteReconcileService`。该服务默认空闲，不在 startup 自动运行，不新增 public MCP tool；`replayPending({ limit, dryRun })` 只读取既有 SQLite reconcile queue，支持 bounded dry-run、`sqlite` / `vector` / `chunks` 显式 replay，成功后按 `memoryId + storeKind` 清理对应 queued tasks；malformed payload、missing memory id、unsupported store kind 或 projection failure 会 fail closed 并保持 queued task 不被清理。CM-1035 temp-local test 使用真实本地 `DiaryStore`、`SqliteShadowStore`、`VectorIndexStore`、`AuditLogStore` 与 `ChunkIndexingService`，先制造一条 synthetic degraded accepted write，再证明 dry-run 不写 projection、不清 queue，随后通过内部 service replay vector/chunk payloads，恢复 vector/chunk projections 与 embedding-cache，并将 reconcile count 降为 `0`；另验证 malformed task 不会被清理、queued sqlite payload 可恢复 SQLite projection、`memory_write_reconcile` 仍不是 public `callTool()`。验证通过：source/app/test syntax checks、CM-1035 targeted test `5/5`、degraded replay/cleanup/restart/write reliability/MCP adjacent regression bundle `22/22`、app-surface regressions `27/27`、full `npm test` `2483/2483`、ledger consistency、docs validation、diff check 与 no-overclaim/public-MCP scans。该 slice 不执行 true live `record_memory`、true live `search_memory`，不读写真实 memory store，不读真实 `.jsonl`，不调用 provider/API，不扩 public MCP，不改 package/config/watchdog/startup，不安装或启动 automatic reconcile worker，不执行 startup reconcile，不执行真实 cleanup/rollback apply，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable`、automatic degraded recovery、real cleanup safe、real rollback safe、governance closure、long-run durability、rollback readiness、RC ready 或 production ready；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。

- `CM-0890 MEMORY_WRITE_PREFLIGHT_CANDIDATE_SOURCE_REVIEW` 已完成 bounded source read-only write-side review：新增 [MEMORY_WRITE_PREFLIGHT_CANDIDATE_SOURCE_REVIEW.md](/A:/codex-memory/docs/MEMORY_WRITE_PREFLIGHT_CANDIDATE_SOURCE_REVIEW.md)。这一步不新增 runtime surface，而是把写入侧 duplicate/idempotence 的当前最小 gap 再收窄一层。审查 `MemoryWriteService`、`MemoryWriteLifecycleDedupSuppressionPreflight`、`SqliteShadowStore`、`CM-0838` runtime integration tests 和 `CM-0835` temp-local duplicate evidence 后，结论已经不该再把重点放在 preflight rule 本身，而应放在 `writePreflightCandidateProvider` 的 exact-scope candidate-source seam。当前仓库现实已经有默认禁用的 internal preflight gate，也已经有 canonical hash / exact scope tuple / fail-closed rejection shape；真正缺的是一个受 review 的 internal `SqliteShadowStore` helper，用 exact target + exact scope tuple 查询最小字段 candidate，而不是复用 `listRecords(target)` 这种 target-wide scan surface。该 review 不扩 public MCP、不改 `callTool()` / `TOOL_DEFINITIONS`、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0889 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_FAMILY_STABILIZATION_REVIEW` 已完成 bounded source read-only family review：新增 [MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_FAMILY_STABILIZATION_REVIEW.md](/A:/codex-memory/docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_FAMILY_STABILIZATION_REVIEW.md)。这一步不再新增 runtime surface，而是把 shared internal runtime-entry gate 的当前仓库现实重新对齐。审查 `InternalRuntimeEntryGate`、`src/app.js`、`ValidateMemoryService`、`TombstoneMemoryService`、`SupersedeMemoryService` 以及三组 runtime-entry regressions 后，结论已经不该再沿用 `CM-0875` 的旧说法。当前 shared internal runtime-entry family 应视为已经稳定收束到 `validate + tombstone + supersede`：三者都具备 default-disabled internal runtime-entry、approved-context enforcement、actor-client derivation、shared normalization，以及对应的 internal service / regression evidence。剩余 blocker 不再是 “supersede 还不属于 shared gate family”，而是 public/runtime durable governance apply、live governance proof 和 readiness/reliability overclaim。`memory_exclude` / `memory_forget` 仍保持 deferred，因为它们仍无 internal runtime service、runtime-entry surface 或 bounded runtime-prep/apply seam。该 review 不扩 public MCP、不改 `callTool()` / `TOOL_DEFINITIONS`、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。

- `CM-0878 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_SHADOW_SEAM_CONTRACT` 已完成 bounded internal helper/fixture/test/docs 收口：新增 [MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_SHADOW_SEAM_CONTRACT.md](/A:/codex-memory/docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_SHADOW_SEAM_CONTRACT.md)、[MemorySupersedeShadowSeamContract.js](/A:/codex-memory/src/core/MemorySupersedeShadowSeamContract.js)、[memory-supersede-shadow-seam-v1.json](/A:/codex-memory/tests/fixtures/memory-supersede-shadow-seam-v1.json) 与 [memory-supersede-shadow-seam-contract.test.js](/A:/codex-memory/tests/memory-supersede-shadow-seam-contract.test.js)。这一步接在 `CM-0877` 后面，把 supersede two-record shadow seam 从纯 review 结论推进成了一个 explicit-input、fail-closed、fixture-only contract helper。当前 helper 不执行任何 runtime 动作，只负责规范 future pair seam 必须声明的最小形状：old/new expectation bundles、双 lifecycle transition、双 link write、shared actor/timestamp/correlation，以及 `singleRecordReuseAllowed=false` 这条关键边界。这样后续 supersede work 就不能再悄悄退回“两次独立单记录 update”这条更弱路径。验证通过：targeted helper test `8/8`。该实现不改 `SqliteShadowStore`、不新增 supersede runtime-prep helper、不新增 internal supersede service、不新增 CLI/runtime entry、不新增 adopter、不扩 public MCP、不改 public `callTool()`、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0877 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_STORAGE_SEAM_REVIEW` 已完成 bounded source read-only storage-seam review：新增 [MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_STORAGE_SEAM_REVIEW.md](/A:/codex-memory/docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_STORAGE_SEAM_REVIEW.md)。这一步接在 `CM-0876` 之后，不再只是说 supersede 还差一个 “runtime-prep 层”，而是进一步把缺口精确化为 storage seam 级别的判断。审查 `SqliteShadowStore.updateLifecycleStatus()`、`ValidateMemoryService`、`TombstoneMemoryService`、supersede projection preview 与 packet contract 后，结论是：如果将来 `memory_supersede` 要进入 internal runtime-prep 或 shared internal runtime-entry gate，它前面首先缺的不是再多一个单记录 helper，而是一个新的 guarded two-record shadow seam。原因很直接：当前 `updateLifecycleStatus(...)` 只覆盖单记录 `memory_id + fromStatus + toStatus + policy guard`，既不会写 `supersedes_memory_id / superseded_by_memory_id`，也不能把 old/new 两条 record 的 lifecycle transition、双向 link、shared metadata 和 correlated success/failure 绑成一个 bounded apply unit。把 supersede 拆成两次独立的 single-record update 会引入 half-applied 中间态，因此不应作为下一个 runtime-prep 基础。最小安全下一步应先是一个 bounded `memory_supersede` two-record shadow-seam contract/design slice，再谈 runtime-prep helper、internal service、CLI/runtime entry 或 shared gate adoption。该实现不新增 adopter、不扩 public MCP、不改 `src/core/constants.js`、不改 public `callTool()`、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0876 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_CANDIDATE_REVIEW` 已完成 bounded source read-only candidate review：新增 [MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_CANDIDATE_REVIEW.md](/A:/codex-memory/docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_SUPERSEDE_CANDIDATE_REVIEW.md)。这一步顺着 `CM-0875` 往下走，但继续保持只读，不直接碰 service 或 gate wiring。审查 `InternalRuntimeEntryGate`、durable governance packet/projection helper、`SqliteShadowStore`、`ValidateMemoryService`、`TombstoneMemoryService` 之后，结论是：`memory_supersede` 虽然已经有 packet contract recognition、projection preview semantics 和 SQLite vocabulary convergence，但它仍然不是 `validate/tombstone` 那种单记录 lifecycle mutation，而是一个双记录、双状态、双向 link 的协调 mutation。当前仓库还没有 internal supersede service、没有 supersede runtime-prep helper，也没有能同时 guard 两条 record policy/lifecycle 并一致写入 `supersedes_memory_id` / `superseded_by_memory_id` 的 two-record shadow seam，因此它现在还不应成为 shared internal runtime-entry gate 的第三个 adopter。最小安全下一步应先是一个 bounded `memory_supersede` runtime-prep / two-record storage-seam review，而不是直接做 service wiring、CLI/runtime entry 或 public MCP 扩口。该实现不新增 adopter、不扩 public MCP、不改 `src/core/constants.js`、不改 public `callTool()`、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0875 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_NEXT_ADOPTER_REVIEW` 已完成 source read-only adopter review：新增 [MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_NEXT_ADOPTER_REVIEW.md](/A:/codex-memory/docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_NEXT_ADOPTER_REVIEW.md)。这一步接在 `CM-0874` 后面，不继续盲目扩 family，而是先把 shared internal runtime-entry gate 的下一个精确 adopter 候选固定下来。审查当前 packet contract、`SqliteShadowStore`、`ValidateMemoryService`、`TombstoneMemoryService` 以及现有 projection/runtime-prep 事实后，结论是：shared gate 现在应继续保持 `validate + tombstone` only。原因是这两条都是已有 service / audit / single-record lifecycle seam 的单记录 mutation；`memory_supersede` 虽然已经有 partial projection semantics，但仍是多记录、双向 link、replacement/current-state coupling 的另一类 runtime problem；`memory_exclude` 和 `memory_forget` 则连 bounded runtime-prep / projection seam 都还没有。因而如果后续要推进第三条 adopter，下一条精确候选应该先是 `memory_supersede` 的 runtime-prep / candidate review，而不是直接把 `exclude/forget` 接进 shared gate。该实现不新增 adopter、不扩 public MCP、不改 `src/core/constants.js`、不改 public `callTool()`、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0874 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_GATE_CONTRACT` 已完成 bounded shared gate contract hardening：新增 [MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_GATE_CONTRACT.md](/A:/codex-memory/docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_RUNTIME_ENTRY_GATE_CONTRACT.md) 与 [tests/internal-runtime-entry-gate.test.js](/A:/codex-memory/tests/internal-runtime-entry-gate.test.js)，并更新 [src/app.js](/A:/codex-memory/src/app.js) 与新增 [src/core/InternalRuntimeEntryGate.js](/A:/codex-memory/src/core/InternalRuntimeEntryGate.js)。这一步把 `CM-0873` 里已经证明可复用的 internal runtime-entry shape 从 “`src/app.js` 里的共享内联逻辑” 收敛成了一个明确的 core helper contract：现在字符串归一化、argument alias 解析、`dry_run` / `confirm`、`actor_client_id` 派生、default-disabled fail-closed、approved internal execution-context gate 都由 `InternalRuntimeEntryGate` 统一承载，而 `app.executeInternalValidate(...)` 和 `app.executeInternalTombstone(...)` 继续复用这层 helper。新增回归验证了 helper 级别的 normalize / alias resolution、disabled fail-closed、approved context requirement 和 accepted payload trim；同时 validate/tombstone runtime-entry 回归仍各自通过 `4/4`。该实现不新增 `validate_memory` 或 `memory_tombstone` public tool、不改 `src/core/constants.js`、不改 public `callTool()` contract、不新增第三条 governance family、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0873 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_VALIDATE_RUNTIME_ENTRY` 已完成 bounded internal validate runtime entry：新增 [MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_VALIDATE_RUNTIME_ENTRY.md](/A:/codex-memory/docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_VALIDATE_RUNTIME_ENTRY.md) 与 [tests/validate-memory-runtime-entry.test.js](/A:/codex-memory/tests/validate-memory-runtime-entry.test.js)，并更新 [src/app.js](/A:/codex-memory/src/app.js)。这一步把 `CM-0872` 的 default-disabled internal runtime-entry gate 证明成了可复用 shape：`src/app.js` 现在有共享 `buildInternalRuntimeEntryPayload(...)` helper，并新增 `app.executeInternalValidate(args, requestContext)`。这条 validate 入口只有在 `internalValidateRuntimeEntryEnabled === true` 且 `requestContext.executionContext.internalValidateRuntimeEntry === true`、`requestSource === internal-validate-runtime-entry` 时才会真正路由到 `app.services.validateMemoryService.validate(...)`；否则 fail-closed。新增回归验证了 default-disabled 拒绝、缺少 approved internal context 拒绝、enabled+approved proposal->active apply 成功、`actor_client_id` 可从 execution context 推导，以及 public MCP tool names 仍保持 `memory_overview / record_memory / search_memory`，`app.callTool('validate_memory', ...)` 仍会 `Unknown tool`。验证通过：`node --test tests\validate-memory-runtime-entry.test.js` `4/4`。该实现不新增 `validate_memory` public tool、不改 `src/core/constants.js`、不改 public `callTool()` contract、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。

- `CM-0868 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_TOMBSTONE_MUTATION_SERVICE` 已完成 bounded internal runtime slice：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_INTERNAL_TOMBSTONE_MUTATION_SERVICE.md`、`src/core/TombstoneMemoryService.js` 与 `tests/tombstone-memory-runtime.test.js`。这一步正好接在 `CM-0867` 之后，把 tombstone-first governance path 从“已有 writable seam 但还缺 service wiring”推进到“已有 internal-only tombstone mutation service，但仍未做 public/runtime wiring”。`TombstoneMemoryService` 复用了 `ValidateMemoryService` 的核心执行形状：schema 校验、secret-like 输入拒绝、lifecycle eligibility、cross-client private guard、默认 `dry_run=true`、`dry_run=false` 时要求 `confirm=true`、pending audit intent、guarded single-record `updateLifecycleStatus(...)`、committed/cancelled audit follow-up。当前允许的状态迁移仍故意保持很窄，只接受 `active/stale/superseded -> tombstoned`。验证通过：`node --test tests\tombstone-memory-runtime.test.js` `14/14`。该实现不把 `memory_tombstone` 暴露为 public MCP tool、不接入 `src/app.js`、不执行 true live memory action、不调用 provider/API，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0867 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_TOMBSTONE_REASON_RUNTIME_SEAM` 已完成 bounded source/test/docs 收敛：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_TOMBSTONE_REASON_RUNTIME_SEAM.md`，并更新 `src/storage/SqliteShadowStore.js` 与 `tests/validate-memory-runtime.test.js`。这一步直接关闭了 `CM-0866` 点名的最小 runtime seam 缺口，但仍然不做 runtime durable governance apply。`SqliteShadowStore.updateLifecycleStatus()` 现在支持 optional `tombstoneReason` 输入，并在 `tombstone_reason` 列存在时把它写入当前单记录 lifecycle path；同时保留原有 `memory_id + from_status`、`client_id / visibility` policy guard、`status_reason`、`lifecycle_updated_at`、`lifecycle_actor_client_id` 行为。验证通过：`node --test tests\validate-memory-runtime.test.js` `16/16`。这意味着当前最小 blocker 已不再是“缺少 writable tombstone_reason seam”，而是仍缺一个 internal tombstone mutation service 来把 packet/dry-run/projection/audit/update 连成真正的 bounded runtime path。该实现不执行 durable governance mutation、不写 governance audit、不做 SQLite apply beyond the existing internal lifecycle seam、不扩 public MCP、不调用 provider/API、不执行 true live memory action，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0866 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_TOMBSTONE_RUNTIME_PREP` 已完成 bounded helper/test/docs 收敛：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_TOMBSTONE_RUNTIME_PREP.md`、`src/core/DurableGovernanceTombstoneRuntimePrepHelper.js` 与 `tests/durable-governance-tombstone-runtime-prep-helper.test.js`。这一步把 `CM-0864` 固定的 “tombstone-first internal-only runtime candidate” 再往前推进一小层，但仍停在 pure internal / zero-side-effect runtime-prep，不做 runtime apply。新 helper 复用 `CM-0862` dry-run preview 与 `CM-0863/CM-0865` projection preview，把 one-packet candidate、one current projection snapshot、one explicit runtime surface capability record 汇合成一个 fail-closed 的 tombstone-first internal apply-plan preview：会生成 pending / committed / cancelled audit event preview、单记录 `updateLifecycleStatus` shadow-update candidate、projected revision token 与 `changedMemoryIds` carry-forward，并显式阻断缺失的 runtime seams。当前-source-like capability 下，helper 会稳定 fail-closed 到 `tombstone_reason_projection_surface_missing`；只有在显式给出完整 runtime surface（包括 writable `tombstone_reason` seam）时，才会输出 coherent 但仍未执行的 internal apply plan。验证通过：targeted runtime-prep helper tests `4/4`。该实现不执行 durable governance mutation、不写 audit、不做 SQLite apply、不扩 public MCP、不调用 provider/API、不执行 true live memory action，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0865 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_PROJECTION_FIELD_CONVERGENCE` 已完成 bounded helper/test/docs 收敛：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_PROJECTION_FIELD_CONVERGENCE.md`，并更新 `src/core/DurableGovernanceShadowProjectionPreview.js` 与 `tests/durable-governance-shadow-projection-preview.test.js`。这一步只做 `CM-0864` 点名的命名收敛缺口，不碰 runtime apply：projection preview helper 现在一方面接受 SQLite 风格输入字段 `status_reason`、`supersedes_memory_id`、`superseded_by_memory_id`、`tombstone_reason`、`lifecycle_updated_at`、`lifecycle_actor_client_id`，另一方面又为现有 logical preview 增补 `beforeSqliteColumns`、`afterSqliteColumns`、`fieldChangesSqliteColumns` 三组 SQLite vocabulary alias surface。这样未来 tombstone-first runtime-prep 或 temp-local/runtime-adjacent proof 不必先手工把 SQLite row vocabulary 改写回旧的 logical field names，但 `CM-0863` 的现有 preview 语义也没有被破坏。验证通过：targeted projection preview tests `7/7`。该实现不执行 durable governance mutation、不写 audit、不做 SQLite apply、不扩 public MCP、不调用 provider/API、不执行 true live memory action，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0864 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_RUNTIME_CANDIDATE_REVIEW` 已完成 source read-only runtime candidate review：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_RUNTIME_CANDIDATE_REVIEW.md`。这一步把 `CM-0860` 到 `CM-0863` 之间仍然模糊的“下一个最小 runtime 候选到底是什么”固定下来。审查确认：`ValidateMemoryService` 已经给出 internal-only governed mutation 的真实参考形状，包括 schema guard、lifecycle eligibility、scope/privacy guard、pending audit intent、guarded SQLite update、committed/cancelled audit follow-up；而 `SqliteShadowStore.updateLifecycleStatus()` 当前仍主要是单记录 `status/status_reason/lifecycle timestamps` 级别的更新接缝，还没有 `supersedes_memory_id` / `superseded_by_memory_id` / `tombstone_reason` 的完整 runtime projection surface。结合 `lifecycle-sqlite-dry-run` 已声明的未来列名与 `CM-0863` projection preview 当前使用的 logical field names，结论是：下一步最小 runtime candidate 应该是 internal-only、tombstone-first、single-record 的路径，而不是先做 `memory_supersede`。`memory_supersede` 仍应保持 deferred，直到双记录 projection、bidirectional links 和命名收敛更明确。该 review 不执行 durable governance mutation、不写 audit、不改 SQLite schema、不扩 public MCP、不做 provider/API/runtime action，也不声明 `memory write reliable`、`memory recall reliable` 或 readiness；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0863 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_SHADOW_PROJECTION_PROOF` 已完成 fixture-backed projection proof：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_SHADOW_PROJECTION_PROOF.md`、`src/core/DurableGovernanceShadowProjectionPreview.js`、`tests/fixtures/durable-governance-shadow-projection-records-v1.json` 与 `tests/durable-governance-shadow-projection-preview.test.js`。这一步把 durable governance mutation 再往前推进一层：在 `CM-0861` packet contract 和 `CM-0862` dry-run preview 之上，新增一个 explicit-input、zero-side-effect、fail-closed 的 shadow projection preview helper。当前只覆盖 `memory_supersede` 和 `memory_tombstone` 两类 bounded projection family：`memory_supersede` 会 preview old record `status -> superseded`、`supersededBy -> newMemoryId`、new record `supersedes -> oldMemoryId` 且 replacement record 进入 `active`；`memory_tombstone` 会 preview target `status -> tombstoned` 并保留 `tombstoneReason`。helper 还会核对 dry-run preview 已接受、projection family 支持、required current projection records 存在、current lifecycle state 合法、exact scope tuple 匹配，以及 link semantics 一致，并输出 deterministic projected revision token 与 changed-memory-id preview。验证通过：targeted projection preview tests `6/6`。该实现不执行 durable governance mutation、不写 audit、不改 SQLite schema、不做 projection apply、不扩 public MCP、不调用 provider/API、不执行 true live memory action、不声明 `memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0862 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_MUTATION_DRY_RUN_HELPER` 已完成 pure internal dry-run helper：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_MUTATION_DRY_RUN_HELPER.md`、`src/core/DurableGovernanceMutationDryRunHelper.js`、`tests/fixtures/durable-governance-mutation-dry-run-request-v1.json` 与 `tests/durable-governance-mutation-dry-run-helper.test.js`。这一步把 `CM-0861` 的 fixture-only packet contract 再往前推进一小层，形成一个 explicit-input、zero-side-effect、fail-closed 的 durable governance mutation dry-run helper。helper 现在会同时核对：contract 是否仍 accepted for planning、mutation family 是否被 `CM-0861` 识别、top-level packet fields 与 family-specific required fields 是否齐全、target cardinality 是否匹配、lifecycle transition 是否完整、scope tuple 是否存在、`validationMode` 是否保持 `internal_dry_run_only`、changed-memory-id policy 是否自洽，以及 mirrored field values 是否与 top-level values 保持一致。preview 输出仍强制 `executionApproved=false`、`runtimeIntegrated=false`、`mutated=false`、`durableAuditWritten=false`、`durableProjectionApplied=false`，并保留 approvals / blockers / changed-memory-id preview / rollback path / audit & projection preview。验证通过：targeted dry-run helper tests `8/8`。该实现不执行 durable governance mutation、不写 audit、不改 SQLite schema、不做 projection apply、不扩 public MCP、不调用 provider/API、不执行 true live memory action、不声明 `memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0861 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_MUTATION_PACKET_CONTRACT` 已完成 fixture-only packet contract：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_MUTATION_PACKET_CONTRACT.md`、`src/core/DurableGovernanceMutationPacketContract.js`、`tests/fixtures/durable-governance-mutation-packet-v1.json`、`tests/durable-governance-mutation-packet-fixture.test.js` 与 `tests/durable-governance-mutation-packet-helper.test.js`。这一步把 `CM-0860` 选定的 durable governance mutation 三段式模型进一步压实成一个 fail-closed 的 explicit-input 合同：packet 现在必须同时说明 mutation family、exact target memory ids、exact scope tuple、actor/request source、reason/evidence、lifecycle transition、audit intent/commit policy、shadow projection policy、revision emitter、changed-memory-ids policy、rollback path、validation mode 与 explicit execution approval statement。`memory_validate`、`memory_supersede`、`memory_tombstone`、`memory_exclude`、`memory_forget` 五类 packet 也都被锁成 internal-only、`BLOCKED_PENDING_APPROVAL`、append-only-audit-required、shadow-projection-required、revision-emission-required、changed-memory-ids-required。验证通过：helper / fixture targeted tests `22/22`。该实现不执行 durable governance mutation、不改 SQLite schema、不写 audit、不扩 public MCP、不调用 provider/API、不执行 true live memory action、不声明 `memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0860 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_MUTATION_FLOW` 已完成 design packet：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_DURABLE_GOVERNANCE_MUTATION_FLOW.md`。这一步没有继续做低价值的 invalidation 微调，而是把 durable governance mutation 的内部主线固定为三段式模型：`append-only governance mutation audit -> SQLite shadow current-state projection -> revision/change-set emitter`。文档明确比较并拒绝了 `inline-only shadow row mutation` 与 `journal-only without projection` 两条路径，选择与当前仓库现实最一致的 hybrid：沿用 `ValidateMemoryService` 的两阶段 audit 心智、沿用 `AuditLogStore` 的 append-only durability、沿用 `SqliteShadowStore` 作为当前治理投影读面，并把 mutation 输出接到 `CM-0852` 到 `CM-0859` 已建好的 revision/change-set invalidation 链。该设计不执行 durable governance write、不改 SQLite schema、不扩 public MCP、不调用 provider/API、不执行 true live memory action、不声明 `memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0859 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_PROVIDER_CHANGESET_INVALIDATION` 已完成 bounded provider-side change-set invalidation：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_PROVIDER_CHANGESET_INVALIDATION.md`，并更新 `src/recall/KnowledgeBaseSyncService.js` 与 `tests/recall-isolation-classification-runtime.test.js`。`governanceStateRevisionProvider` 现在除了 legacy scalar/string revision 和 `{ revision, entries }` snapshot 之外，也兼容 `{ revision, changedMemoryIds }` 的 sparse change-set 形态；当 provider 明确给出 `changedMemoryIds` 时，custom provider path 可以在 governance-only drift 时直接按这些 `memoryId` 精准清除 candidate cache，而不必每次都提供 full snapshot。snapshot path 仍可用，legacy scalar path 仍保留 fail-closed target-family fallback。验证通过：changed source/test syntax checks 与 `node --test tests\recall-isolation-classification-runtime.test.js`（`26/26`）。该实现不新增 durable governance store、不强制 provider 必须实现 sparse delta/full snapshot、不做 user/agent/folder projection、不做 candidate-generator pre-ranking governance rewiring、不执行 true live memory action、不读取真实 memory 或 real `.jsonl` / durable content、不调用 provider/API、不写 durable memory/audit、不做 cleanup apply / rollback apply、不扩 public MCP、不声明 `memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0858 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_PROVIDER_SNAPSHOT_PER_RECORD_INVALIDATION` 已完成 bounded provider-side per-record invalidation：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_PROVIDER_SNAPSHOT_PER_RECORD_INVALIDATION.md`，并更新 `src/recall/KnowledgeBaseSyncService.js` 与 `tests/recall-isolation-classification-runtime.test.js`。`governanceStateRevisionProvider` 现在兼容两种 internal 形态：legacy scalar/string revision 仍维持原有 fail-closed target-family invalidation；如果 provider 返回 `{ revision, entries }`，则 custom provider path 也能像 default governance path 一样保存 per-record governance snapshot，并在 governance-only drift 时按变更的 `memoryId` 精准清除 current-fingerprint candidate cache。验证通过：changed source/test syntax checks 与 `node --test tests\recall-isolation-classification-runtime.test.js`（`25/25`）。该实现不新增 durable governance store、不强制 provider 一定实现 per-record snapshot、不做 user/agent/folder projection、不做 candidate-generator pre-ranking governance rewiring、不执行 true live memory action、不读取真实 memory 或 real `.jsonl` / durable content、不调用 provider/API、不写 durable memory/audit、不做 cleanup apply / rollback apply、不扩 public MCP、不声明 `memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。

- `CM-0852 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_GOVERNANCE_SYNC_TOKEN_HOOK` 已完成 bounded internal sync/cache hook：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_GOVERNANCE_SYNC_TOKEN_HOOK.md`，并更新 `src/recall/KnowledgeBaseSyncService.js`、`src/recall/KnowledgeBaseRecallPipeline.js`、`src/recall/CandidateGenerator.js` 与 `tests/recall-isolation-classification-runtime.test.js`。`KnowledgeBaseSyncService` 现在支持 optional internal `governanceStateRevisionProvider`，`syncTarget()` 会返回 `governanceStateRevision`，`buildSyncToken()` 会在 revision 非空时把它编码进去；`KnowledgeBaseRecallPipeline.search()` 会把该 revision 继续传给 `CandidateGenerator.generate()`，而 `CandidateGenerator.buildCacheKey()` 也会在 revision 非空时把它编码进 candidate-cache key。验证通过：changed source/test syntax checks 与 `node --test tests\recall-isolation-classification-runtime.test.js`（`14/14`）。这意味着未来 durable governance state 一旦落地，就能改变 recall sync/cache addressing，而不必先扩 public MCP。该实现仍是 bounded/internal hook，不创建 durable governance state、不做 governance-only eager cache flush、不做 user/agent/folder projection、不做 candidate-generator pre-ranking governance rewiring、不执行 true live memory action、不读取真实 memory 或 real `.jsonl` / durable content、不调用 provider/API、不写 durable memory/audit、不做 cleanup apply / rollback apply、不扩 public MCP、不声明 `memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0851 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_CANDIDATE_CACHE_INVALIDATION_REVIEW` 已完成 source read-only review：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_CANDIDATE_CACHE_INVALIDATION_REVIEW.md`。审查确认 `CM-0850` 的 internal/default-disabled post-result lifecycle/scope governance bridge 仍会在 candidate-cache hit 之后执行，所以当前 candidate-cache reuse 不会绕过 governance filtering；但 `CandidateGenerator` cache key 和 `KnowledgeBaseSyncService.buildSyncToken()` 目前只编码 query shape、candidate filters、embedding fingerprint、context signature、isolation-classifier version 和 diary sync state，并未编码未来 durable governance-state revision。结论是：一旦后续实现 proposal / approval / supersession / tombstone / forget 等 durable governance mutation，仍需要 sync-token/cache-key enrichment 或 explicit bounded invalidation rules，之后才适合讨论更深的 candidate-generator governance rewiring。该 review 不实现 cache invalidation、不实现 durable governance state、不覆盖 user/agent/folder projection、不执行 true live memory action、不读取真实 memory 或 real `.jsonl` / durable content、不调用 provider/API、不写 durable memory/audit、不做 cleanup apply / rollback apply、不扩 public MCP、不声明 `memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。
- `CM-0850 MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_RUNTIME_INTEGRATION` 已完成 bounded runtime integration：新增 `docs/MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_RUNTIME_INTEGRATION.md` 与 `tests/memory-lifecycle-scope-runtime-integration.test.js`，并更新 `src/app.js`、`src/core/MemoryLifecycleScopeGovernanceContract.js`、`src/storage/SqliteShadowStore.js`。`search_memory` 现在有一个 internal/default-disabled post-result lifecycle/scope governance bridge，仅在 `requestContext.executionContext.lifecycleScopeGovernanceReadPolicy === true` 时启用；public `search_memory` args 和 public MCP tools 不变。bridge 通过 exact `memoryId` metadata lookup 获取 lifecycle/scope 字段，不读取 raw memory content，并复用 CM-0844/CM-0845 helper 过滤 proposal / malformed / out-of-scope 等候选，suppressed metadata 不复制 raw `content` / `text` / `title` / `snippet` / `sourceFile` / `.jsonl` 字段。验证通过：新 bridge test `3/3`，相邻 lifecycle/read-policy regression `20/20`。该实现仍是 bounded/internal/default-disabled，不执行 true live memory action、不读取真实 memory 或 real `.jsonl` / durable content、不调用 provider/API、不写 durable memory/audit、不做 cleanup apply / rollback apply、不扩 public MCP、不声明 runtime lifecycle governance complete、`memory write reliable` 或 `memory recall reliable`；`RC_NOT_READY_BLOCKED` 保持不变。

## 下一个目标

- 长期目标现在收束为：把 `codex-memory` 推进成默认可用、可审计、可回滚、可治理、VCP 兼容的本地优先 memory runtime。
- 第一大阶段是可靠性闭环：证明 `memory recall reliable`、证明 `memory write reliable`、把 bounded evidence 推进到受控 live evidence，同时避免 readiness / reliability overclaim。
- 第二大阶段是治理闭环：落地 memory proposal / approval / supersession / tombstone / forget flow，明确 user/project/agent/task/client/workspace scope，并防止错误、陈旧、越界、rejected、tombstoned 或 superseded memory 长期污染 recall。
- 近期执行顺序应从可靠性闭环继续，同时进入治理闭环入口：mainline reconciliation / patched metadata-only recall boundary 状态同步已由 `CM-0831` 完成；write reliability proof matrix 已由 `CM-0832` 完成；fixture-only write matrix evidence 已由 `CM-0833` 落地；synthetic temp-local write evidence 已由 `CM-0834` 落地；scope / duplicate / pollution evidence 已由 `CM-0835` 落地；lifecycle / dedup / suppression preflight contract 已由 `CM-0836` 落地；runtime integration candidate review 已由 `CM-0837` 完成；最小 optional runtime integration 已由 `CM-0838` 完成；bounded integration review 已由 `CM-0839` 完成；rollback / cleanup posture review 已由 `CM-0840` 完成；rollback / cleanup bounded evidence plan 已由 `CM-0841` 完成；fixture-only rollback / cleanup bounded evidence 已由 `CM-0842` 完成；lifecycle/scope governance plan 已由 `CM-0843` 完成；fixture-only lifecycle/scope governance contract 已由 `CM-0844` 完成；read-policy fixture evidence 已由 `CM-0845` 完成。下一步只能在 separately exact approval 下进入 CM-0825 patched true live proof / future exactly-one write proof，或继续做 `MEMORY_LIFECYCLE_SCOPE_TEMP_LOCAL_EVIDENCE_PLAN`、candidate-provider source review、temp-local lifecycle evidence；不做真实 memory scan / live write / cleanup apply / readiness claim。
- 写入侧当前最近的安全结论是：`CM-0896` 已把 future live write proof 里最容易滑坡的 duplicate-basis discovery 也固定住了。也就是说，`CM-0892/CM-0893` 形成的 opt-in app seam 不仅被 `CM-0894` 重新定性为 internal-only operational seam、被 `CM-0895` 固定为唯一对齐消费路径，而且被 `CM-0896` 明确要求 future proof 必须预绑定 exact duplicate basis，不能 broad scan、不能 `search_memory`、也不能用双写去制造证据；但在那之前，仍不应把这条 seam 视为 default runtime behavior，也不应把 temp-local evidence 误读成 `memory write reliable`。
- 非目标保持不变：不追求 `RC_READY`，不做 release/deploy/cutover，不扩 public MCP，不做 migration/import/export/backup/restore apply，不把 provider-backed runtime validation 设为默认常态。

- `CM-0737 StoreWAsk execution and preflight repair` 已完成本地实现：用户第一次明确批准 `StoreWAsk` 后，本轮按 preflight `approvalPacket.proposedArguments` 走本地 HTTP MCP authorized `tools/call` 执行一次 `record_memory`，结果为 HTTP `200` 但 tool `decision=rejected`，未返回 `memoryId`；只读 audit tail 显示拒绝原因是 `process memory must include checkpoint, risk, todo, pending, or stage-conclusion.`。随后修复 `src\cli\store-freshness-write-preflight.js`，让 proposed `process` 记忆的 title/content 明确包含 `Checkpoint` 信号，并在 `tests\store-freshness-write-preflight-cli.test.js` 中用 `validateProcessEntry()` 锁定 proposed payload 可被 process-memory 规则接受。用户第二次明确批准修正后的 `StoreWAsk` 后，本轮再次且仅一次执行 `record_memory`，结果为 HTTP `200`、tool `decision=accepted`、`memoryId=codex-process-1ef539a197d747e199e12fe1c0d69731`、`shadowWrite.status=ok`。只读复核显示 store 从 `3 records / 8 chunks` 变为 `4 records / 9 chunks`，`last24h=1`、`last7d=4`，preflight 决策变为 `STORE_FRESHNESS_EVIDENCE_NOT_REQUIRED`，dashboard `goalReadiness.blockers` 已移除 `store_freshness_evidence_not_written`，但仍保持 `LOCAL_MEMORY_MAINLINE_NOT_READY / NOT_READY_BLOCKED`。边界：本轮总计仅两次由用户分别明确批准的 `record_memory` MCP calls，第一次 rejected、第二次 accepted；未执行 `search_memory`、provider/API call、config/startup change、remote action、additional write、push、release、deploy、cutover 或 readiness claim。验证已通过：`node --check src\cli\store-freshness-write-preflight.js`、`node --check tests\store-freshness-write-preflight-cli.test.js`、`node --test tests\store-freshness-write-preflight-cli.test.js`（`4/4`）、真实 preflight/dashboard/audit smoke、`npm test`（`1970/1970`）、docs validation、v3 parser smoke、`git diff --check`。
